BUYER BEWARE!!! Read This Review! TIJUANA offers a better shopping experience & products than this place!

When I purchased them, I was given a specific day that they would be ready and marked it on my calendar. I scheduled my work in that area and waited for a call. About 3 o‚Äôclock rolled around and they never called and I had to leave the area. I finally called them and they told me they were not going to be ready for pickup for another couple days. I had the loaner stools loaded up in my truck and had to drive back to Miramar during rush hour traffic to drop off the stools, which costed me lost work time. The glides (pads on each leg so that the floor does not get damaged) on the bottom of the stools were installed by their warehouse and were falling off as well. We did not even take the time to open the other boxes. We brought them back, they said they would address all the issues and call us when they arrived... A day, a week, a month.... who knows?  When they were finally repaired by the factory, they were then shipped to the warehouse to put the glides on the bottom of the legs. They again, let them cure for a day which is how long they said the glue needs to sit and dry for, then delivered them and the pads were still not glued on. One came off and ruined my carpet with a black glue stain (see photo). The delivery guy didn‚Äôt even care or apologize. Also the fabric was cut poorly showing foam through the seams. They wanted us to keep the stools as is and did not even offer money off! What a joke. We refused delivery and they brought them back to the warehouse and on their 3rd try did it right. This 3rd time costed me a whole day of sitting around waiting for 2 separate deliveries on a Saturday that I had plans to take my family somewhere for the day. The fact we were not even offered money back really makes me mad. By the time we got the stools it was almost 2 months when it was supposed to be 2 weeks max. They damaged the carpet, and even told me they wanted me to keep them after the original delivery which would have destroyed our brand new LVP flooring. Completely botched our whole experience.<//text>

< review>
I have two chef knives that I put through the ringer almost every single day. I am not a chef, but just a guy who likes to cook at home and save money by doing so. One damascus knife is a no-name brand, but my Wusthof knife was a dream when I initially got it. Overtime, I could tell that the knife was losing its sharpness, to make matters worse, my significant other accidentally snapped the tip off, just a small piece. I saw Perfect Edge on Yelp a couple months ago and put it off until I really couldn't stand my dull knives anymore.

Honestly, I don't know why I waited so long. For the price and how quickly it got taken care of, I would make this a regular part of my routine. Both my knives came back perfect. The Wusthof knife had its tip repaired and I could not tell you the last time I was able to slice onions, garlic, tomatoes, so thin without effort.

I will definitely be coming back in the future and be referring friends here. I just suggest you give a call ahead to get a timeline for when you can get your blades back.

**This review is in regards to my experience with dropping the knives off at East Sacramento Hardware in Sacramento, CA.<//review>

<rate>5< /rate>< text>
Wow,  this park is right up there with Dennis the Menace park in Monterrey. There was several different sections to the park (dog park,  tennis court,  half court for basketball,  enclosed toddler section, larger area for the older kids,  and a grassy area to walk around). It was busier than expected,  but everyone had their mask on (except for young toddlers).  The more unique aspect of the park was the Treasure Hunt and Scavenger Hunt.  The kids had a lot of fun looking for the stuff there while playing on all the slides.  My boys are 4 and their cousins are 6 and 8, respectively; everyone had a lot of fun running around.  It was great that all the kids and parents there was respective of others. Would highly recommend this park.</text>

< Text>
Wonderful park for toddlers and elementary age kids. There is a fenced in area with sand, slides, and swings. There is a splash pad that is open in the summertime and there is an area with a pirate ship for older kids. There is also a basketball court and tennis court and an area with grills and a bathroom. This park can get very busy during the summer and the parking lot is very small. I usually park on the street and walk to the park. The only reason this park doesn‚Äôt get a five star review is because parking can be difficult.<//Text>

<pictures>None< /pictures>< Text>
I have been going since its grand opening. If you play Ingress, the park has portals about every 10 feet. Designed for kinds, lots of safety features such as padded rubber floors in the main activity area. Good for small group picnics. Restrooms in the center, basketball and tennis courts near the street. Unfortunately the parking lot only hold half a dozen cars, and another 7 or 8 might fit on-street. Not nearly enough. There is a tiny dog park section, just a sand floor. Big grassy area is sometimes co-opted by non-city organized activities.< /Text>

<resp>None</resp>< Text>
One of the best parks we have been visiting . Our 5 year old has been going since she was 2 and has not got bored yet. Play area & structures are recently built (few years). Lots of kids - regardless of time of day. There is a cool water area that is operational during spring and summer time. There is a seperate fenced toddler area with sand boxx , swings and slides.

There is also a very nice fenced dog park next to it. Finally, there is a basketball court and a wide open park to throe ball around.

Parking can at times be a pain due to limited space but you can always find space on the road<//Text>
